msg:Environment: The hotel is located between the mountains and lakes, very secluded and beautiful; the lake and mountain scenery is absolutely beyond words, and the empty mountains are even more beautiful after the rain, which makes people feel extremely calm!
Hygiene: The hygiene needs to be improved. The carpets and elevators in the guest room public area are poorly maintained and look old. The tablecloths in the breakfast room are also a bit stained, and the table mat is a piece of house sale advertising paper! ğŸ¤”
Service: The service is quite satisfactory. It was already 11:30 pm when we arrived very late, and it was raining heavily. The shuttle driver pointed us to the guest room because the shuttle bus was charging. It occupies a large area here, but it is still easy to find different buildings along the different colored lines on the ground
Facilities: The facilities in the room are very similar to those of an apar**ent. It is indeed built according to the standards of house sales. The lake view is very good, and the room is huge. It would be nice to add a bathtub in such a large area, but apar**ents are generally not designed like this.
The key point is that the tram friendliness here is average. I searched for Nanjing Nengrui's fast charging piles and found that all five were closed. Three of them were at the bottom of the slope near the Internet-famous Lake Center Pavilion, and they were broken and had no power. The two on the right hand side of the parking lot at the entrance of the hotel lobby were temporarily closed. Fortunately, there are slow charging piles in the parking lot of the guest room building, about five or six in number, with an electricity price of 1.26. The key is that the charging is extremely slow, 7kw. It is best to make an appoin**ent for charging at night, and there will be a place fee for overtime recycling. This place is not marked on the map. I have added relevant information about the wheat power station on Gaode for everyone. You can consider charging during the day unless the car is temporarily unused.
Overall, the experience is good and worth recommending. The external scenery is better than the internal management
